Move the selection to previous line wrap point, or failing that to the start of the line. 

If the line is indented, and the cursor isn\textquotesingle{}t already at the end of the indentation, this will move to the end of the indentation instead of the start of the line. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2commands_2dist_2index_8js_aa5c66d1445e89670321e4a6f050173a5}\label{_0dcodemirror_2commands_2dist_2index_8js_aa5c66d1445e89670321e4a6f050173a5}}

The default keymap. 

Includes all bindings from \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#commands.standardKeymap}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily standard\+Keymap}}} plus the following\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Alt-\/\+Arrow\+Left (Ctrl-\/\+Arrow\+Left on mac\+OS)\+: \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#commands.cursorSyntaxLeft}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily cursor\+Syntax\+Left}}} (\href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#commands.selectSyntaxLeft}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily select\+Syntax\+Left}}} with Shift)
\item Alt-\/\+Arrow\+Right (Ctrl-\/\+Arrow\+Right on mac\+OS)\+: \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#commands.cursorSyntaxRight}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily cursor\+Syntax\+Right}}} (\href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#commands.selectSyntaxRight}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily select\+Syntax\+Right}}} with Shift)
\item Alt-\/\+Arrow\+Up\+: \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#commands.moveLineUp}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily move\+Line\+Up}}}
\item Alt-\/\+Arrow\+Down\+: \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#commands.moveLineDown}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily move\+Line\+Down}}}
\item Shift-\/\+Alt-\/\+Arrow\+Up\+: \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#commands.copyLineUp}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily copy\+Line\+Up}}}
\item Shift-\/\+Alt-\/\+Arrow\+Down\+: \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#commands.copyLineDown}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily copy\+Line\+Down}}}
\item Escape\+: \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#commands.simplifySelection}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily simplify\+Selection}}}
\item Ctrl-\/\+Enter (Comd-\/\+Enter on mac\+OS)\+: \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#commands.insertBlankLine}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily insert\+Blank\+Line}}}
\item Alt-\/l (Ctrl-\/l on mac\+OS)\+: \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#commands.selectLine}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily select\+Line}}}
\item Ctrl-\/i (Cmd-\/i on mac\+OS)\+: \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#commands.selectParentSyntax}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily select\+Parent\+Syntax}}}
\item Ctrl-\/\mbox{[} (Cmd-\/\mbox{[} on mac\+OS)\+: \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#commands.indentLess}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily indent\+Less}}}
\item Ctrl-\/\mbox{]} (Cmd-\/\mbox{]} on mac\+OS)\+: \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#commands.indentMore}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily indent\+More}}}

The state field used to store the history data. 

Should probably only be used when you want to \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#state.EditorState.toJSON}{\texttt{ serialize}} or \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#state.EditorState^fromJSON}{\texttt{ deserialize}} state objects in a way that preserves history. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2commands_2dist_2index_8js_a4c1e373a75251c6d1d4b453f09d216a4}\label{_0dcodemirror_2commands_2dist_2index_8js_a4c1e373a75251c6d1d4b453f09d216a4}}

This facet provides a way to register functions that, given a transaction, provide a set of effects that the history should store when inverting the transaction. 

This can be used to integrate some kinds of effects in the history, so that they can be undone (and redone again). \mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2commands_2dist_2index_8js_a6fb2b7e9ba30bc573832ee67408d6483}\label{_0dcodemirror_2commands_2dist_2index_8js_a6fb2b7e9ba30bc573832ee67408d6483}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily const isolate\+History = \mbox{\hyperlink{classAnnotation_ae50507c0109a9afd9538801d63a1398d}{Annotation.\+define}}()}



\mbox{\hyperlink{classTransaction}{Transaction}} annotation that will prevent that transaction from being combined with other transactions in the undo history. 

Given {\ttfamily \char`\"{}before\char`\"{}}, it\textquotesingle{}ll prevent merging with previous transactions. With {\ttfamily \char`\"{}after\char`\"{}}, subsequent transactions won\textquotesingle{}t be combined with this one. With {\ttfamily \char`\"{}full\char`\"{}}, the transaction is isolated on both sides. \mbox{\Hypertarget{_0dcodemirror_2commands_2dist_2index_8js_aa7bd5a49690db5320d576ee4e71e28e2}\label{_0dcodemirror_2commands_2dist_2index_8js_aa7bd5a49690db5320d576ee4e71e28e2}}

An array of key bindings closely sticking to platform-\/standard or widely used bindings. 

(This includes the bindings from \href{https://codemirror.net/6/docs/ref/\#commands.emacsStyleKeymap}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily emacs\+Style\+Keymap}}}, with their {\ttfamily key} property changed to {\ttfamily mac}.)
